<text>I feel I need to give a little bit of background in order to explain the gravitas of the work Tom and John at Land Rover Carlsbad put into making this deal happen.

I was raised by a car salesman, so let's say that my dad taught me a few things about how to close a deal, but more importantly, taught me the effort these professionals put into making someone's dream come true, and Tom and John were no exception.

A week ago I got my first car, and I got my dream car, that car you catch yourself seeing at every corner, and imagining yourself driving it, that's the car I got - A Range Rover EVOQUE!!

The process was long and extensive until I met Tom. I had been negotiating with dealerships all the way from Fresno to San Diego (I am local to Los Angeles), but from the moment I got on a call with Tom, he said two things that struck me, "I won't lose this deal, and I will make sure you will have the best experience." The hour had not passed before Tom had called me back with a deal that blew every single other dealership out of the water. It was such a crazy deal, that I asked my father (the car salesman) to drive up to Carlsbad for two things, to check if the deal was real or if they would change it up on me, and if it was to not lose it! When my dad got there 4 hours later (due to work), he called me to say that I needed to get there and sign the paperwork. ¬†I am not kidding, what had taken me 3 months with other dealerships, took me exactly 24 hrs between picking up the phone and driving out with my new car.

Tom is simply the best salesman I have ever met, he is dedicated, trustworthy, and will bend over backward to get you what you are looking for. If you have ever thought about getting a car, especially a range rover, please trust me and go with him, NO ONE ELSE. You will never get a better deal or better customer service, he supported me and my family through this process.

You can check my profile, I normally don't write reviews, but this was too great of an experience for me to not say something.

I also have to give a shout out to John, from the financing team who, beyond being one of the funniest and most charismatic individuals I have ever met, made it possible with my very limited budget to get everything a young man needs on their first car. He made my monthly payment accessible, and included every perk and discount he could find, in order for me to drive out with that car. The conversations I had with John were beyond just the car and more about life and how to be. The deal, although it was the best in the State, was just a perk to who he was.

I conclude this review by saying that, my family and I left in tears, because as an immigrant family, to have their son's first car to be a Range Rover Evoque, encompasses a series of challenges we have overcome as a family to make it one step closer to the American dream.

I thank everyone at Range Rover Carlsbad for this opportunity, I won't ever forget the day I got my first car.</text>< Resp>

We recently had our vehicle at Hoehn Land Rover for service.  The front parking sensors were extremely sensitive and going off all the time.  Initially we were told that the front bumper had been impacted causing the camera and sensor to have shifted/moved.  Our vehicle has not been in a collision or accident, but Hoehn Land Rover says they can prove that our vehicle has hit something causing the damage.

I initially went to pickup our vehicle on a Monday, one week after it was dropped off for service.  My wife was initially told it would be ready to be picked up on Tuesday, however they vehicle was not done on time because the service advisor told my wife they do not have enough technicians to service the vehicles. <username>David Temple< /username><review>THIS is what EVERY car-buying experience should look and feel like. I could stop there and you'd likely get the picture; however, there is so much more to say. First of all, if you're looking for a vehicle that is not only among the very finest made, but offers more safety factors than you can shake a nine iron at, the Land Rover lineup is the brand to shop. Secondly, the fit and finish on the Discovery Sport HSE is like a hand-tailored suit; it's smooth and refined, well-appointed, and offers the sort of head-turning attention it deserves. Thirdly, and I don't know about you, but better than 50% of my (and my wife's) pleasure of buying (or leasing) comes in the EXPERIENCE we get when shopping, dining, traveling, etc. And Jaguar-Land Rover Carlsbad is exactly the sort of experience you're looking for and expect from a Top Shelf dealership. Experience is Everything, and the team at JLRC make it happen in style. Lastly, and perhaps my favorite part of our recent experience, is Tom Wallace. Tom is the Business Manager & Sales Person who assisted us. I reached out to Tom weeks, if not months ago, when we first began our homework. He responded professionally, and without being pushy, letting me know in a confident way that he would be there for me when the right moment came. That moment came this past week. And by the weekend, we were driving away with a vehicle that, while I had dreamed of having such a vehicle, has exceeded my expectations in many ways. Yes, I have had a Rover in the past. In fact, I had a Range Rover Sport. Moreover, it quickly became my favorite. Personally, and as much I like the RR Sport, I believe this is a much better fit for me and my wife. The "Disco" is smaller, more fuel efficient--thanks to the lighter weight, and is equally luxurious (and for $10-20K less). Besides, the HSE has all the same bells & whistles and is much friendlier to the wallet (in gas consumption). But back to the best part of the experience: Tom Wallace. Tom is the consummate professional. His charming and helpful demeanor is simply outstanding. His attention to detail, knowledge of both the vehicles and the financing is superb. Finally, it's his warmth that makes you leave the lot feeling like you have a new friend--one that you can rest assured has Got Your Back. All that rambling said (you can't stop an enthusiastic writer from sharing), you owe it to yourself to (a) consider a ROVER for your next luxury purchase, (b) consider shopping Jaguar Land Rover Carlsbad (instead of nearby San Diego), and (c) consider asking for "our new friend" Tom Wallace. <Rate>5</Rate>< Review>
Dr. Costa is a wonderful person who truly cares about people & her patients dental health. She doesn't just assume you know what a procedure entails & tries to explain everything to you as she is going along. She's also not afraid to give with the Novacaine.
I am a difficult patient because I have many health issues, medications I take & strange allergies, almost all with severe reactions. Today I saw Her for an emergency visit after a 3 1/2 year hiatus in which I had been being seen at Western Dental in Antioch. She not only warmly welcomed me back with open arms & a waiting chair (She stayed late to be able to see me.) She didn't scold me for allowing my teeth to come to such a pass. She was just glad to have me back in her care & able to help. Even though my leaving previously had been a bit strained & many years had passed, she & the staff were warm, caring & asked about my family as if it has only been a few weeks instead of a few years! They even remembered my daughter's & my then newborn granddaughter's names! Also, though I'm fairly certain it's noted in the computer, they knew who my husband was & his dental issues even though we have different last names.
All this babbling to basically say, I think Dr. Costa is a kind, warm, caring, well educated Dentist who's genuinely concerned about not just you're dental health but your overall health & welfare, WITHOUT being nosy! A fantabulous combination that's hard to find... The Office Staff as well. Definitely gonna stay with her from now on!<//Review>

<Review>4 STAR. Overall. Would return but gotta make sure to specify no MSG otherwise it's just on par with other cantonese restaurants. Love the refillable complimentary free soup though. Not your average cheap free soup. My 7 year old had 2 bowls of that, paired with rice, and called it a meal. Generous portion at an average of $8 to $10 per plate to share. Ordered about one dish per person to share and still have plenty to take home.

Other: On the salty side in general. Some dishes are pre-MSG-ed. Avoid where makes sense. Fast service. Wouldn't be opposed to dine here if chosen by my group of friends. Just double emphasize the no MSG. Newly opened less than a month ago, doing well so far. <Text>I had a wonderful experience here with my mom, and besides the food being wonderful, the staff were wonderful too. I had kashk-e badamjan, dolma, beef soltani, and zereshk polo. The dolma (a filling wrapped in grape leaves and stewed) were my mom's favorite and I loved the kashk-e badamjan (an eggplant dip made with dried, fried mint, fried onions, and topped with keshk, which is a salty fermented whey product, a Persian analog to yogurt). The beef soltani, which is tri-tip and koobideh (ground meat formed around a skewer and cooked) was very yummy and very generous. The chicken was perfectly cooked in the zereshk polo (a dish made with saffron and burberries - somewhat like a dried cranberry, sour and sweet) and very tender and juicy. .The service was on point as well. It was really soooo good. It's an awesome surprise to find such good Persian food in the valley!<//Text></record>

Affordable, terrific sushi from lovely friendly people<//review>

<username>Dominique Vance< /username><Rating>5</Rating></record></dataset><record>
< user_id>
108145579792989251982</user_id>
< user_name>
Hal Lutsko< /user_name>
< time>
1535008358638</time>
< Rate>
5</Rate>
< text>
To give fair warning to anyone going in the first time: It's required to order a minimum of 4 items per person at a table and 5 per person if sitting at the bar. Sitting at the bar also means that the chef decides what you eat.

With that caveat out of the way the sushi was absolutely the best I've ever had. Many of the dishes had sauces put into them while being made and were recommended to be eaten without anything added to them. I followed that advice and didn't regret it for a moment.

The fish melted in the mouth and, even as a person who enjoys spicy foods but doesn't handle them well, the spicy sauce put into each item was superbly done and never caused me any problems. Each individual part was designed to perfectly compliment the main ingredient.

I do have to specifically mention that the eel was stunningly delectable and now heads my "best sushi item ever" list.

The staff was incredibly nice and unfailingly polite even though I came in a bare 30 minutes before they closed. The restaurant was small but delightfully proportioned to allow close seating without feeling crowded. The place seemed quite clean and well kept, the music selection was nice and provided excellent background to the idle talk, and the location makes it into a hidden gem nestled between other businesses.

I highly recommend this place for anyone looking to delight their palate and appreciate a small and quiet meal. I personally intend to make a more regular habit of visiting.< /text>

< Review>
First of all make sure you are truly ready for this visit.  Prepare by leaving your phone in your car for sure!  Do not be fooled, chef is old school and does not tolerate disruptions from beyond his establishment.  I wouldn't either if I was creating excellence and making dreams come true.   His chefs choice selection is ordered from the sushi bar and can be ordered from the few tables available.  But if you choose the bar a "thank you chef" or " I am full chef" is all to be said.  He doesn't need the engagement while creating perfection.  Chef Murata brings the craftsmanship of a true master to the quality of LA's freshest fish in a humble establishment maintained by his closest family.  Please be respectful, bring an appetite, and remember LEAVE THE PHONE IN YOUR CAR!  At the table you can order from the menu if you have specific taste, but he has never served anything less that Wow!  Sit back, enjoy, and take it in.  By no means a steal, but definitely a bargain compared to your LA, NYC, and Vegas options.  The freshness, quality, and skill for a modest price.  Don't expect to spend less than $50 unless you are portion controlling.  But I don't when I dine there.  I eat until "just one more" and I'm done :)<//Review>

< text>
Delicious food, with a very pleasing aesthetic.

Update 4/5/18:
On second visit the dinner was fairly bland. The menu was ambitious, but the dishes lacked flavor. I had a chicken stuffed with feta and sun-dried tomato, and my girlfriend had a beef pasta, both seemed like they were salt deficient and the pasta was overcooked.

Our appetizers were also fairly ambitious, hers was a bitter greens salad with prosciutto and a duck egg in which the flavors didn't quite mix. Mine was a mandarin and fennel salad that had good flavor but was very limp.

The wine selection was great, and the cider was quite delicious.

We did not have any desserts because they were out of the panna cotta at 7pm. The other desserts looked like they could be good, but just weren't appealing to us.

Overall, it was quite a let down tonight after being so great the first time as went in. However, the aesthetic is still nice and the sourdough focaccia they served upon seating us was delicious.< /text>

< review>
Small neighborhood park in the heart of Normal Heights/Kensington. Love to bring my dog here for socializing and also very nice quiet and clean park to just hang out and walk around.

The gated in soccer field is used by dog owners to play fetch with their dogs or just let them run around and socialize with other doggos.

Park has restroom facilities and tables for picnics and open spaces for picnics and kiddos to run around.<//review>

Nice clean open park, close to a busy street but its closed off by a small fence (around 3ft6in high I'd say). Two playgrounds, one for smaller kids and the other for older kids. <user_name>Justin Lee Arn< /user_name><date>1480412032464<//date>< Response>

<userid>100961015519520042976< /userid><rating>3</rating>< Text>
Having just moved to the neighborhood, I was delighted to discover Ward Canyon Park within walking distance of my house. The park is very large, consisting of a acres of grassy fields, and built in their area, children's play apparatus, and happily, a dog park!
There are several good grilling posts for bbqs and the park was quite green from all of the recent rains.

My only concern regards the clearly apparent homeless population that takes residence in the park. While walking on the path I spied several tents and a few areas of the park had trash buildup. The people I came across were nice, however and I'll be returning tomorrow with my dog to have some fun at the dog park.</Text>
<pics>None<//pics></record></dataset><record>
<user>107002596731281414790< /user>< Text>
Of the five parks I regularly visit, this one is my favorite. Two distinct jungle gyms (which split comfortably along age lines when the park is busy), bathroom (with junkies in it only occasionally), hoops, two sets of swings, clean water fountains, two attached off leash dog parks, and a huge wide open grassy area. The trees while bare in the winter provide great shade to make Ward Canyon tolerable even in the heat waves of september. I like the extreme diversity of families that visit here.  Weekends there's always multiple parties and bounce houses, and the mornings are dominated by kids under 5 while the median age grows as the day progresses. Sometimes they do free movies in the park here and watching Princess Bride with 3000 neighbors was a highlight.</Text>
